3975<h1>

3976How to Design a Modern Farmhouse Kitchen</h1>

3977

3978

3979<p>

3980&nbsp;</p>

3981

3982

3983<h6>

3984By Mikael Short</h6>

3985

3986

3987<h6>

3988September 23, 2021</h6>

3989

3990</div>

3991</div>

3992</div>

3993</div>

3994</div>

3995</div>

3996</div>

3997</div>

3998</div>

3999</div>

4000</div>

4001</div>

4002</div>

4003<div class="">

4004<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-af-d--de-fbbaad">

4005<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-af-d--de-fbbaad">

4006<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

4007<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

4008<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

4009<div class="">

4010<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-fe-d-a-eb-adbecb">

4011<div class="merce-column-container">

4013<div>

4014<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4015<div>

4016<p>

4017<em>

4018We interviewed multiple design professionals to create guides about the most popular interior design styles. After you&rsquo;ve finished with modern farmhouse design, check out other styles on the Vevano Home <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/category/design-101/">

4019Design 101</a>

4020. If you like modern farmhouse, you may also be interested in <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/home-interior-styles-transitional-design/">

4021transitional design</a>

4022.</em>

4023</p>

4024

4025

4026<p>

4027Want the charm of a traditional farmhouse kitchen with the sophistication of <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/home-interior-styles-minimalist-design/">

4028minimalist design</a>

4029 and modern functionality? If so, you&rsquo;ve come to the right place. With the help of expert interior designers, we&rsquo;ve outlined everything you need to know about designing the perfect modern farmhouse kitchen for your home.</p>

4030

4056<div>

4057<h2>

4058What Is Modern Farmhouse Style?</h2>

4059

4060</div>

4061</div>

4062</div>

4063</div>

4064<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-aaf-bf---fcdbbfaaf">

4065<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf aaf-bf---fcdbbfaaf-singleImageAlignment">

4066<img class="aaf-bf---fcdbbfaaf-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/Z5fx2IbYNdgU4QZHM5H20VfXnAGjtJfIY3jCfZKOl4s/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9tb2Rlcm4tZmFybWhvdXNlLWtpdGNoZW4tZGVzaWduL21vZGVybi1mYXJtaG91c2Uta2l0Y2hlbi1pZGVhLmpwZw" alt="Modern farmhouse kitchen featuring white modern shaker cabinets" title="Modern farmhouse kitchen featuring white modern shaker cabinets"/>

4067</div>

4068</div>

4069<div class="">

4070<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-dee-c--ae-fefeb">

4071<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-dee-c--ae-fefeb">

4072<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

4073<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

4074<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

4075<div class="">

4076<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-ebd-e-de-ad-edbfc">

4077<div class="merce-column-container">

4078<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-ecea-d--ab-fdbba">

4079<div>

4080<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4081<div>

4082<p>

4083<span style="color:#000000;">

4084<span style="font-size:20px;">

4085<em>

4086&ldquo;Think of modern farmhouse as a contemporary spin on traditional farmhouse. So you&rsquo;ll have some traditional farmhouse elements like an apron sink, but you&rsquo;ll also have something modern and trendy, like black matte finishes.&rdquo;</em>

4087</span>

4088<span style="font-size:18px;">

4089<em>

4090&mdash;</em>

4091<strong>

4092Michael, Vevano Home Designer</strong>

4093</span>

4094</span>

4095</p>

4103</div>

4107</div>

4112<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4113<div>

4114<p>

4115At its core, the modern farmhouse style has the foundation of traditional farmhouse style&mdash;practicality and comfort, focusing on natural elements&mdash;topped off with modern designs and features. Modern farmhouse design balances the clean, streamlined approach of contemporary styles with warm, rustic callbacks to traditional farmhouse decor.</p>

4117</div>

4143<h3>

4144Modern Farmhouse vs. Traditional Farmhouse</h3>

4145

4146

4147<p>

4148The traditional farmhouse style encourages warmth by using natural elements&mdash;wood, iron, metal, etc.&mdash;and vintage features to create a cozy yet practical feel. Traditional farmhouse design might be described as &ldquo;shabby chic&rdquo; or&nbsp;because the style often incorporates aged or antique decor for a more inviting, homey interior&mdash;similar to <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/cottage-style-decor-interior-design/" target="_blank">

4149cottage interior design</a>

4150.</p>

4151

4152</div>

4153</div>

4154</div>

4155</div>

4156<div class="">

4157<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-efa-e--af-cec">

4178&nbsp;displays minimal details and&nbsp;modern finishes.</em>

4225<div>

4226<p>

4227The traditional farmhouse style is less uniform than modern or contemporary styles, which relies on straight, clean lines and a minimalist, form-follows-function approach to design.</p>

4228

4229

4230<p>

4231Modern farmhouse takes the traditional farmhouse style and makes it more streamlined with cleaner lines since the <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/home-interior-style-modern-design/">

4232modern style</a>

4233 focuses more on simple and functional features. Modern farmhouse styles are unique in that you may find a blend of modern, industrial, and contemporary design choices to create a truly unique kitchen that maintains the warmth desired from farmhouse designs.</p>

4260<div>

4261<h2>

4262Modern Farmhouse Kitchen Characteristics &amp; Design Tips</h2>

4263

4264</div>

4265</div>

4266</div>

4267</div>

4268<div class="">

4269<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-ebf-ef-de-b-cbdca">

4270<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-ebf-ef-de-b-cbdca">

4271<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

4272<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

4273<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

4274<div class="">

4275<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-bbdb-a-b-ac-cefddf">

4276<div class="merce-column-container">

4277<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-da-b--bd-ceef">

4278<div>

4279<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4280<div>

4281<p>

4282<em>

4283<span style="font-size:20px;">

4284&ldquo;You can approach modern farmhouses in a couple of different ways. You can buy items that are a blend of modern and farmhouse (think modern Shaker cabinets), or you could have a traditional&nbsp;fixture paired with fully&nbsp;contemporary designs, like having a very rustic farmhouse light in a kitchen with modern frameless cabinets.&rdquo;</span>

4285</em>

4286 <em>

4287<span style="font-size:18px;">

4288&mdash; </span>

4289</em>

4290<strong>

4291<span style="font-size:18px;">

4292Michael, Vevano Home Designer</span>

4293</strong>

4294</p>

4295

4296</div>

4297</div>

4298</div>

4299</div>

4300</div>

4301</div>

4302</div>

4303</div>

4304</div>

4305</div>

4306</div>

4307</div>

4308</div>

4309<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-aeed-fd-d-ac-facfdd">

4310<div>

4311<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4312<div>

4313<p>

4314With a focus on a blend of natural elements, colors, simple designs, and rustic or even industrial touches, the modern farmhouse has a variety of options available regarding features that will bring out a unique modern farmhouse aesthetic.</p>

4315

4316</div>

4317</div>

4318</div>

4319</div>

4320</div>

4321</div>

4322</div>

4323</div>

4324</div>

4325</div>

4326</div>

4327</div>

4328</div>

4330<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-a--b-a-afebc">

4336<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-fc--a-aa-edcfec">

4341<div>

4342<h3>

4343Colors</h3>

4344

4345</div>

4346</div>

4347</div>

4348</div>

4349<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-ca-fb--fc-abfa">

4350<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf ca-fb--fc-abfa-singleImageAlignment">

4351<img class="ca-fb--fc-abfa-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/JIGA2W5n5G36k8rGB0YEVlN0H2OPZf1ZPJlKufNo8d8/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9tb2Rlcm4tZmFybWhvdXNlLWtpdGNoZW4tZGVzaWduL21vZGVybi1mYXJtaG91c2Uta2l0Y2hlbi1ncmF5LWNhYmluZXRzLmpwZw" alt="modern farmhouse kitchen featuring a light gray color scheme and farmhouse sink" title="modern farmhouse kitchen featuring a light gray color scheme and farmhouse sink"/>

4352</div>

4353</div>

4354<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-ec-cd--a-cfaecb">

4355<div>

4356<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4357<div>

4358<p>

4359The modern farmhouse color scheme features mainly whites, blacks, grays, and other neutral tones. Wood tones are also popular as its timber was commonly used in traditional farmhouse designs, light or dark.</p>

4360

4361

4362<p>

4363For pops of color, shades from the outside world work best to keep with a natural theme: navy blue, robin&rsquo;s egg blue, sage green, forest green, sunny yellow, etc.</p>

4364

4365

4366<p>

4367The trick for modern farmhouse colors is to find the right balance between warm and cool tones. If the kitchen has almost all warm tones, it will feel more like a traditional farmhouse style. On the other hand, if all the shades are cold, the kitchen may look too modern (natural wood floors or fixtures would warm it up). That&rsquo;s why natural elements like wood flooring or cabinets help to soften up the modern farmhouse look.</p>

4368

4369</div>

4370</div>

4371</div>

4372</div>

4373</div>

4374</div>

4375</div>

4376</div>

4377</div>

4378</div>

4379</div>

4380</div>

4381</div>

4383<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-aad-eea--ae-bab">

4384<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-aad-eea--ae-bab">

4385<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

4386<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

4418<h3>

4419Cabinets</h3>

4420

4421</div>

4422</div>

4423</div>

4424</div>

4425<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-dfa-b-fc-c-adcbbbd">

4426<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf dfa-b-fc-c-adcbbbd-singleImageAlignment">

4427<img class="dfa-b-fc-c-adcbbbd-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/kiT5knT5lq175DD27LZzhGEJcBeoE0F0731PzAA46dw/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9tb2Rlcm4tZmFybWhvdXNlLWtpdGNoZW4tZGVzaWduL3NoYWtlci13aGl0ZS1jYWJpbmV0cy1tb2Rlcm4tZmFybWhvdXNlLWtpdGNoZW4uanBn" alt="Modern farmhouse kitchen featuring shaker white cabinets" title="Modern farmhouse kitchen featuring shaker white cabinets"/>

4428</div>

4429</div>

4430<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-bce-df-fb-cbf-beddd">

4431<div>

4432<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4433<div>

4434<p>

4435Modern <a href="https://vevano.com/page/farmhouse-kitchen-cabinets/">

4436farmhouse kitchen cabinets</a>

4437 typically run in the middle of the lane in terms of style: not too minimalist in design, but not too much detail either. For this reason, modern Shaker style cabinets are popular in modern farmhouse kitchens because of their sleek, contemporary twist on the traditional recessed door style.</p>

4438

4439

4440<p>

4441Though traditional Shaker doors often included rounded bevels or glazed panels, the modern Shaker cabinet keeps it simple, offering up clean lines and minimal detailing that&rsquo;s better suited to a modern-leaning farmhouse kitchen.</p>

4442

4444</div>

4446</div>

4460<p>

4461<em>

4462<span style="font-size:20px;">

4463&ldquo;The white modern Shaker cabinets give you a good base. Then, from there you can add in little decor pieces whether it&rsquo;s a rug or artisan pots for more of the farmhouse.&rdquo;</span>

4464</em>

4465<span style="font-size:18px;">

4466<em>

4467&mdash;</em>

4468<strong>

4469Madi, Vevano Home Designer</strong>

4470</span>

4471</p>

4473</div>

4474</div>

4475</div>

4476</div>

4477</div>

4478</div>

4479</div>

4480</div>

4481</div>

4482</div>

4483</div>

4484</div>

4485</div>

4486<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-faed-c-ed-dfa-afeabc">

4487<div>

4488<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4489<div>

4490<p>

4491For the staple modern farmhouse look in your kitchen, white <a href="https://vevano.com/product/32044-sww10x10-shaker-white-10x10-kitchen/">

4492Shaker style cabinets</a>

4493 seal the deal. Though white is the most popular choice, cabinets in <a href="https://vevano.com/product/32041-sdd10x10-shaker-dove-10x10-kitchen/">

4494Shaker Dove</a>

4495 or <a href="https://vevano.com/product/32043-sgg10x10-shaker-grey-10x10-kitchen/">

4496Shaker Grey</a>

4497 also work well.</p>

4498

4499

4500<p>

4501For those who seek a more traditional farmhouse style for cabinets, <a href="https://vevano.com/product/32030-cww10x10-cobbleridge-white-10x10-kitchen/">

4502Cobbleridge White</a>

4503 cabinets have just enough detailing to hit the mark without too much embellishment to be considered truly traditional.</p>

4504

4505

4506<p>

4507Another option for cabinetry in modern farmhouse kitchens is open wooden shelving so you can show off your collection of vintage dishware in an accessible and stylish way.</p>

4508

4523A way to add modern contrast and intrigue to your modern farmhouse kitchen would be to have <a href="https://vevano.com/page/dark-kitchen-cabinet-collections/" target="_blank">

4524dark cabinets</a>

4525 highlighted either on your base cabinets or island cabinets, surrounded or topped with white Shaker cabinets.</p>

4528<h4>

4529<span style="font-size:20px;">

4530What to Avoid</span>

4531</h4>

4532

4533

4534<p>

4535Cabinets like <a href="https://vevano.com/product/32033-eaw10x10-eastland-antique-white-10x10-kitchen/">

4536Eastland Antique White</a>

4537 may lean too far traditional in terms of embellishment and color. On the other end of the spectrum, <a href="https://vevano.com/product/32038-mcw10x10-monte-carlo-gloss-white-10x10-kitchen/">

4538Monte Carlo Gloss</a>

4539 may lean too far modern with its slab design and glossy finish.</p>

4590<h3>

4591Countertops</h3>

4592

4593

4594<p>

4595Our designers recommend a couple <a href="https://vevano.com/page/countertops/">

4596types of countertops</a>

4597 to fit the modern farmhouse style.</p>

4598

4599

4600<p>

4601Andrea recommends a beautiful and hardy white or gray quartz countertop, especially one with a grayish-blue vein. A cooler undertone for countertops will help balance any warmth from a wood-look floor or other wooden features to master the blend of farmhouse and modern.</p>

4777<h3>

4778Lighting</h3>

4779

4780</div>

4781</div>

4782</div>

4783</div>

4784<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-d-a---bbaa">

4785<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf d-a---bbaa-singleImageAlignment">

4786<img class="d-a---bbaa-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/csyM3r3m5rW7k-ADhjDQVrMEGrxoiaK5EFjME4CGo00/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9tb2Rlcm4tZmFybWhvdXNlLWtpdGNoZW4tZGVzaWduL21vZGVybi1mYXJtaG91c2Uta2l0Y2hlbi1saWdodGluZy5qcGc" alt="Modern farmhouse kitchen lighting" title="Modern farmhouse kitchen lighting"/>

4787</div>

4788</div>

4789<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-cbbba-c--be-bccbf">

4790<div>

4791<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4792<div>

4793<p>

4794There is a range of ideal lighting fixtures for modern farmhouse style, depending on whether you want the lighting to be a statement piece or simply serve its function. Overall, our designers highlight lighting that fits farmhouse or <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/home-interior-styles-industrial-design/">

4795industrial styles</a>

4796 or are modern minimalistic.</p>

4797

4798

4799<p>

4800When it comes to <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/pendant-lighting-kitchen-islands/">

4801pendant lighting over your kitchen island</a>

4802, our designers recommend the <a href="https://vevano.com/product/39527-e24916-bksbr-fungo-235-single-pendant-in-black/">

4803black dome pendant</a>

4804 or a <a href="https://vevano.com/product/39596-2644bkab-capitol-125-four-light-linear-pendant-in-black-and-antique-brass/">

4805linear pendant</a>

4806 to highlight function while still having a simple modern style.</p>

4807

4808

4809<p>

4810For more farmhouse lighting styles, consider what may have been in farmhouses back in the day&mdash;like lanterns and candles. Lantern lighting fixtures are particularly popular for modern farmhouse kitchens.</p>

4811

4830<em>

4831<span style="font-size:20px;">

4832&ldquo;In terms of lighting, you could go a lot of different ways because the modern farmhouse is a transitional space between multiple styles. You could do something industrial, like the black iron, or you could do something more modern with brushed nickel</span>

4833</em>

4835<span style="font-size:20px;">

5023<h3>

5024Hardware</h3>

5025

5026

5027<p>

5028Vevano Home&rsquo;s expert designers assert that simple pulls or knobs are popular in modern farmhouse kitchens. The <a href="https://vevano.com/product/17035-7876-1vb-463-traditional-cup-pull-in-verona-bronze-from-vibrato-collection/">

5029cup pulls</a>

5030 and half-dome pulls in particular lend to the modern farmhouse appeal nicely.</p>

5031

5032

5033<p>

5034In terms of color and finish, matte black, oil-rubbed bronze, and brushed nickel are standard for the modern farmhouse style. Bronze, in particular, can pop beautifully surrounded by white and gray, adding that touch of warmth.</p>

5035

5036

5037<p>

5038Don&rsquo;t be afraid to mix metals in terms of finishes in your kitchen, our designers say! That fits well within the warm and vintage farmhouse style.</p>

5039

5040

5041<h4>

5042<span style="font-size:20px;">

5043What to Avoid</span>

5044</h4>

5045

5046

5047<p>

5048Anything too decorative or elaborate in hardware may come across as too traditional. Too much oil-rubbed bronze may also trend more traditional if the kitchen isn&rsquo;t furnished in a more modern fashion.</p>

5049

5050</div>

5051</div>

5052</div>

5053</div>

5054</div>

5055</div>

5099<h3>

5100Flooring</h3>

5101

5102</div>

5103</div>

5104</div>

5105</div>

5106<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-e--d--baeec">

5107<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf e--d--baeec-singleImageAlignment">

5108<img class="e--d--baeec-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/xwWM7e0lSdfshC1HiL-L239KvDFdlXVWbgfEE6_kbUw/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9tb2Rlcm4tZmFybWhvdXNlLWtpdGNoZW4tZGVzaWduL21vZGVybi1mYXJtaG91c2Uta2l0Y2hlbi13b29kLWZsb29yaW5nLmpwZw" alt="wood flooring in white modern farmhouse kitchen" title="wood flooring in white modern farmhouse kitchen"/>

5109</div>

5110</div>

5111<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-ae-ff-b-aec-abcf">

5112<div>

5113<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

5114<div>

5115<p>

5116Since modern farmhouse kitchens lean on natural elements, any wood look would be ideal for flooring.</p>

5117

5118

5119<p>

5120That could include engineered <a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/flooring-hardwood/">

5121hardwood floors</a>

5122, tile, <a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/flooring-luxury-vinyl-tile/">

5123luxury vinyl tile</a>

5124,&nbsp;or <a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/flooring-laminate/">

5125laminate flooring</a>

5126 that&rsquo;s designed to look like wood. Light or dark wood would work well for a modern farmhouse kitchen, depending on the rest of the kitchen&rsquo;s design.</p>

5127

5128

5129<p>

5130Andrea also suggests that big slate or slab tiles that look like marble in cool tones could also contribute to a modern farmhouse feel.</p>

5131

5132

5134<span style="font-size:20px;">

5135What to Avoid</span>

5136</h4>

5137

5138

5139<p>

5140While travertine tiles are very beautiful, they lend themselves to more of a Tuscan or traditional style than to a modern farmhouse style.</p>

5191<h3>

5192Backsplash</h3>

5193

5194</div>

5195</div>

5196</div>

5197</div>

5198<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-eb-ebe--ab-dca">

5199<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf eb-ebe--ab-dca-singleImageAlignment">

5200<img class="eb-ebe--ab-dca-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/TxYtprl1co20m-EMqH406mBvzGEgO--kVzbw28ZbswA/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9tb2Rlcm4tZmFybWhvdXNlLWtpdGNoZW4tZGVzaWduL2hleGFnb24tYmFja3NwbGFzaC1mYXJtaG91c2Uta2l0Y2hlbi5qcGc" alt="farmhouse kitchen with hexagonal tile backsplash" title="farmhouse kitchen with hexagonal tile backsplash"/>

5207<p>

5208Simple backsplash tiles are the most befitting of the modern farmhouse aesthetic. This could be <a href="https://vevano.com/product/1327-mami164-133-brick-subway-mosaic-with-white-tiles-114-x-12-sheet/">

5209white subway tiles</a>

5210 or <a href="https://vevano.com/product/1469-pibl23-hexagon-fabric-textured-ceramic-patchwork-mosaic-with-white-tiles-12-x-104-sheet/">

5211white hexagonal tiles</a>

5212. For a little more character, handmade artisan tiles can make for a beautiful backsplash. If you decide to go for a design, make sure the tones correspond with your chosen color scheme.</p>

5213

5214

5215<p>

5216In sticking with natural elements, sometimes brick might be a fun addition to a modern farmhouse kitchen, particularly when painted white.</p>

5363Sinks</h3>

5364

5365</div>

5366</div>

5371<img class="bfcb-b-bd-bb-aef-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/4yRcxXZIwxUi2i3e6WwxLYOjqB9XFWgvWLIj2KnKr1U/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9tb2Rlcm4tZmFybWhvdXNlLWtpdGNoZW4tZGVzaWduL21vZGVybi1mYXJtaG91c2Uta2l0Y2hlbi1zaW5rLmpwZw" alt="Farmhouse kitchen sink" title="Farmhouse kitchen sink"/>

5378<p>

5379A signature feature of modern farmhouse kitchens is the <a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/sinks-kitchen-farmhouse/">

5380farmhouse kitchen sink</a>

5381, also known as an apron-front sink. Usually, in white ceramic or porcelain, the timeless farmhouse sink can handle the mess and prep of large loads while maintaining a nostalgic feel.</p>

5382

5383

5384<p>

5385Nowadays, it&rsquo;s not uncommon to see a copper or bronze farmhouse sink too, but white is the classic favorite to achieve the farmhouse aesthetic with ease.</p>

5386

5387

5388<p>

5389If not a farmhouse sink, a white <a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/sinks-kitchen-undermount/">

5390undermount kitchen sink</a>

5391 would also fit a modern farmhouse look.</p>

5562gourmet kitchen </a>

5563with a farmhouse twist. A traditional <a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/faucets-kitchen-bridge/">

5564bridge kitchen faucet</a>

5565 might also work well in a modern farmhouse kitchen as long as it&rsquo;s balanced with more contemporary features.</p>

5716<h3>

5717Finishing Touches</h3>

5718

5719

5720<p>

5721Since the way to soften up a <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/kitchen-layout-ideas/" target="_blank">

5722modern kitchen layout</a>

5723 is through the eclectic and vintage details that are signature to farmhouse styles, stylistic touches like rugs, art, plant life, and other decor are sure to help you achieve the modern farmhouse look you like.</p>

5724

5725

5726<p>

5727Vintage or thrifted decor can lend itself well to the mismatched farmhouse style, so you can focus on modern cabinetry or lighting to balance modern lines with rustic touches.</p>

5728

5756<span style="font-size:20px;">

5757Range Hood</span>

5758</h4>

5759

5760

5761<p>

5762One way to make a statement is to have a decorative cover for your range hood to match or work with your cabinets. Beadboard covers for range hoods have become popular for modern farmhouse kitchens.</p>

5790<h4>

5791<span style="font-size:20px;">

5792Art</span>

5793</h4>

5794

5795

5796<p>

5797Any painted artwork, especially landscapes or nature-oriented pieces that look like they would fit in a farmhouse, would highlight the farmhouse aesthetic. Neutral or cool colors in paintings or photographs will help the artwork blend into the modern farmhouse kitchen more naturally.</p>

5798

5799

5800<p>

5801Photographs of farm animals are also a good option for modern farmhouse kitchens.</p>

5802

5803

5804<p>

5805Avoid bright-colored or contemporary abstract paintings as those will contrast too much with the modern farmhouse style.</p>

5833<h4>

5834<span style="font-size:20px;">

5835Rugs</span>

5836</h4>

5837

5838</div>

5844<img class="ebab-f--a-ce-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/AKQN-g38R1vgeCWcCylcwpPCBnRBS5VbkFOF3DjIjKk/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9tb2Rlcm4tZmFybWhvdXNlLWtpdGNoZW4tZGVzaWduL3NtYWxsLW1vZGVybi1mYXJtaG91c2Uta2l0Y2hlbi5qcGc" alt="rug in a modern farmhouse kitchen" title="rug in a modern farmhouse kitchen"/>

5845</div>

5846</div>

5847<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-fd-ec--abe-def">

5849<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

5850<div>

5851<p>

5852<a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/furniture-decor-rugs/">

5853Rugs</a>

5854 with a natural (or faux) material or pattern are great for adding texture and warmth to a modern farmhouse kitchen. For example, a <a href="https://vevano.com/product/37172-smat-001a-harland-rug-in-warm-brown-60-x-05-x-84/">

5855cow-hide rug</a>

5856 will definitely tap into a rustic farmhouse feel, or this <a href="https://vevano.com/product/37173-iwil-057-indigo-rug-in-indigo-108-x-05-x-144/">

5857indigo rug</a>

5858 will add a nice touch of color to an otherwise neutral modern farmhouse style.</p>

5859

5860

5861<p>

5862Note that rugs that are too brightly colored or boldly patterned might clash with a modern farmhouse kitchen.</p>

6162<div>

6163<h2>

6164Is Modern Farmhouse Going Out of Style?</h2>

6165

6166

6167<p>

6168The modern farmhouse style is more in style than ever, thanks to popular design TV shows that lean heavily on modern farmhouse styles in their designs and renovations. And the popularity makes sense. Modern farmhouse is an excellent blend of timeless traditional features and clean, modern lines that make it easily transitional and flexible with other styles.</p>

6169

6170</div>

6171</div>

6172</div>

6173</div>

6174<div class="">

6175<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-ab-a-c-ac-dfabbf">

6176<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-ab-a-c-ac-dfabbf">

6177<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

6178<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

6179<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

6180<div class="">

6181<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-bbbe-dc-dc-bb-bda">

6182<div class="merce-column-container">

6183<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-bd--b-ba-edd">

6184<div>

6185<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

6186<div>

6187<p>

6188<em>

6189<span style="font-size:20px;">

6190&ldquo;It has more of that transitional element, so the modern farmhouse kitchen can evolve over time. The clean, modern white Shaker cabinets or rustic hardwood floor can work with other styles in the future if you don&rsquo;t want to keep the modern farmhouse.&rdquo;</span>

6191<strong>

6192<span style="font-size:20px;">

6193 </span>

6194</strong>

6195<span style="font-size:18px;">

6196&mdash;</span>

6197</em>

6198<span style="font-size:18px;">

6199<strong>

6200&nbsp;Madi, Vevano Home Designer</strong>

6201</span>

6202</p>

6203

6204</div>

6205</div>

6206</div>

6207</div>

6208</div>

6209</div>

6210</div>

6211</div>

6212</div>

6213</div>

6214</div>

6215</div>

6216</div>

6217<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-dcce-c-b-ab-dfabc">

6218<div>

6219<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

6220<div>

6221<p>

6222As with any trend, some are more popular than others, and some have longer lifetimes than others thanks to their classic or timeless appeal&mdash;much like the farmhouse style.</p>

6223
